FACILITY   (SYNCH,3CPRIHP) Back-n facility of the China           3285600100024 
           Spallation Neutron Source (CSNS)                       3285600100025 
INC-SOURCE (SPALL) The neutron beam is produced through the       3285600100026 
           pulses of protons with an energy of 1.6 GeV and a      3285600100027 
           pulse frequency of 25 Hz, bombarding a tungsten        3285600100028 
           target. The Back-n white neutron beamline is           3285600100029 
           constructed 180 degree to the proton beam direction,   3285600100030 
           and the neutron flux can reach up to 1E7 n/cm2/s at    3285600100031 
           the experimental station.                              3285600100032 
DETECTOR   (SCIN) The Back-n C6D6 detector system consists of     3285600100033 
           four C6D6 liquid scintillation detectors, one          3285600100034 
           aluminum detector's brackets, and one aluminum sample  3285600100035 
           holder. The C6D6 detectors are placed upstream of the  3285600100036 
           neutron beam sample target to decrease the elastic     3285600100037 
           scattering neutron background, and the detector axis   3285600100038 
           is at an angle of 110 degree from the neutron beam.    3285600100039 
           The distance between the C6D6 detectors front center   3285600100040 
           to the sample target center was 150 mm and 80 mm from  3285600100041 
           the neutron beam axis.                                 3285600100042 
           (SI) SiMon detector for detection of triton and alpha  3285600100043 
           from 6Li(n,t+a) reaction.                              3285600100044 
SAMPLE     The gold sample (Au) with a diameter of 50 mm, a       3285600100045 
           thickness of 1 mm, a weight of 37.93 g and an area of  3285600100046 
           19.63 cm2. The area density is 0.005907 atoms/barn.    3285600100047 
METHOD     (TOF) The length of neutron flight path is             3285600100048 
           approximately 76 m.                                    3285600100049 
           (PHWT) Weighting function calculated by Geant4.        3285600100050 
MONITOR    Absolute normalization to the 4.9 eV saturated         3285600100051 
           resonance.                                             3285600100052 
           (3-LI-6(N,T)2-HE-4,,SIG) for shape normalization       3285600100053 
CORRECTION The factor fc was introduced for considering the       3285600100054 
           multi-elastic scattering of neutrons in the thick      3285600100055 
           sample, which is related to the absorption cross       3285600100056 
           section and the thickness of the sample. It is the     3285600100057 
           ratio of the mean neutron transmission length to the   3285600100058 
           target thickness.                                      3285600100059 
ANALYSIS   Capture cross section derived from the capture yield   3285600100060 
           multiplied by the ENDF total cross section (sigma)     3285600100061 
           and divided by the absorption correction factor        3285600100062 
           1-exp(-n*t*sigma*fc), n is the density of the sample,  3285600100063 
           t is the thickness of the sample, fc is the fixed      3285600100064 
           factor of the sample thickness.                        3285600100065 
ERR-ANALYS (ERR-T) Total uncertainty                              3285600100066 
           (ERR-S,,2.) The statistical uncertainty, < 2%.         3285600100067 
           (ERR-1) The energy dependence of the neutron flux,     3285600100068 
           about 5%.                                              3285600100069 
           (ERR-2,2.,3.) Pulse height weighting technique, 2~3%.  3285600100070
